title: "HoTT exercises"
date: "2018-04-08"

categories: type-theory
toc: true
---

This is a self-contained version of some solutions for HoTT-Book's exercises.
The idea is to unpackage all as long as possible to get a better understanding.
Many changes can appear running this experiment. Solutions are
type-checked as a whole using Agda v2.5.3.

## Requirements

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Agda has a pragma to work with HoTT:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="527" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="531" class="Keyword">OPTIONS</a> <a id="539" class="Option">--without-K</a> <a id="551" class="Symbol">#-}</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Equality type definition also called Identity type:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="714" class="Keyword">infix</a> <a id="720" class="Number">4</a> <a id="722" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#731" class="Datatype Operator">_≡_</a>

## Chapter 1

### Exercise 1.1

{: .exercise}
  Given functions $$f : A \to B$$ and $$g:B\to C$$, define
  their composite $$ g\circ f:A\to C$$.
  Show that we have $$h \circ (g\circ f) \equiv (h\circ g)\circ f$$.


We define the composition operation in Agda as follows.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="_∘_"></a><a id="2124" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2124" class="Function Operator">_∘_</a> <a id="2128" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2130" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="2132" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2133" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2133" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="2135" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2135" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="2137" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2137" class="Bound">k</a><a id="2138" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="2140" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2141" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2141" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="2143" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2145" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="2149" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2133" class="Bound">i</a><a id="2150" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="2152" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2152" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="2154" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2156" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="2160" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2135" class="Bound">j</a><a id="2161" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="2163" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2163" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="2165" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2167" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="2171" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2137" class="Bound">k</a><a id="2172" class="Symbol">}</a>
    <a id="2178" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2180" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2181" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2152" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="2183" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2185" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2163" class="Bound">C</a><a id="2186" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="2192" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2194" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2195" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2141" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="2197" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2199" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2152" class="Bound">B</a><a id="2200" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="2206" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2208" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2141" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="2210" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2212" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2163" class="Bound">C</a>
<a id="2214" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2214" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="2216" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2124" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="2218" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2218" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="2220" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="2222" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="2224" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2224" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="2226" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2228" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2214" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="2230" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2231" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2218" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="2233" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2224" class="Bound">x</a><a id="2234" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Then, the `∘-assoc` shows us that associativity of this composition holds.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="∘-assoc"></a><a id="2337" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2337" class="Function">∘-assoc</a> <a id="2345" ### Exercise 1.2

<div class="exercise">
Derive the recursion principle for products $$\mathsf{rec}_{A\times B}$$
using only the projections, and verify that the definitional equalities
are valid. Do the same for $$\Sigma$$-types.
</div>

To solve this problem we need to know:

  - The recursion principle for Σ-types:

    <p class="equation">
    $$ \mathsf{rec}_{ A \times B}
      : \prod\limits_{C : \mathcal{U}} (A \to B \to C) → A \times B \to C.
    $$
    </p>

  - The recursion principle for Σ-types:

    <p class="equation">
    $$ \mathsf{rec}_{\sum\limits_{(x : A) } B(x)}
      : \prod\limits_{(C : U)} (\Pi_{(x : A)} B(x) \rightarrow C) \rightarrow
        \sum_{(x : A)} B(x) \rightarrow C
    $$
    </p>

<div class="proof" id="proof-1.2">
Proof.<br/>
For products:<br/>
If we have the projections,
$$\mathsf{proj}_1 : A \times B \to \mathsf{A}$$ and $$\mathsf{proj}_2 : A \times B \to \mathsf{B}$$,
then $$\mathsf{rec}_2$$ is another inhabitant where

<p class="equation">
$$
\begin{align*}
&\mathsf{rec}_1 : \prod\limits_{C : \mathcal{U}} (A \to B \to C) \to A \times B \to C\\
&\mathsf{rec}_1~C~g~c~:\equiv~g~(\mathsf{proj}_1 c,~\mathsf{proj}_2 c).
\end{align*}
$$
</p>
By reflexivity, we prove the equality between $$\mathsf{rec}_{ A \times B}$$ and $$\mathsf{rec}_1$$.
<br/>
<br/>
For sums:<br/>
The projections are $$\mathsf{proj}_1 : \sum_{x : A}  Bx \to \mathsf{A}$$ and
$$\mathsf{proj}_2 :  \prod_{(p : \sum_{x : A}  Bx)} \to \mathsf{B} (\mathsf{proj}_1 p)$$.<br/>
By using these projections, we got another recursor defined as follows:
<p class="equation">
$$
\begin{aling*}
&\mathsf{rec}_2 : \prod\limits_{C : \mathcal{U}}  (\prod_{x : A} Bx \to C) \to \sum\limits_{x : A} B x \to C\\
&\mathsf{rec}_2~C~g~c~=~g~(\mathsf{proj}_1 c)~(\mathsf{proj}_2 c)
\end{align*}
$$
</p>

By reflexivity, we prove the equality between $$\mathsf{rec}_{\sum\limits_{(x : A) } B(x)}$$ and $$\mathsf{rec}_2$$.
</div>

the following exercises including this one:

that we provide.

  <a id="Σ-Rec₁.rec"></a><a id="5387" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#5387" class="Function">rec</a> <a id="5391" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5393" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4941" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="5395" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#5258" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="5397" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#5269" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="5399" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5401" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#5284" class="Bound">C</a>

  <a id="5487" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#5438" class="Function">rec-β</a> <a id="5493" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#5493" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="5495" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#5495" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="5497" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5499" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#779" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

On the other hand, the product type is just a particular case of the sigma type
when the codomain is not dependent, as we can see next by omitting the argument
in `(λ _ → B)`.

Its recursor with a function $$g : A \rightarrow B \rightarrow C$$ that we provide.

### Exercise 1.3

<p class="exercise">
Derive the induction principle for products $$\mathsf{ind}_{A\times B}$$,
using only the projections and the propositional uniqueness principle
$$\mathsf{uniq}_{A\times B}$$.
Verify that the definitional equalities are valid.
</p>

To solve this problem, recall the uniqueness principle (Pp. 29. HoTT-Book)

- The **propositional uniqueness principle** says that
every element of $$A\times B$$ is equal to a pair.

<p class="equation">
  $$ \mathsf{uniq}_{A\times B}
     : \prod_{(x : A \times B)} ((\mathsf{proj}_{1}(x) , \mathsf{proj}_{2}(x))
       \equiv_{A\times B} x).
  $$
</p>

Product type definition using `data`:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="6956" class="Comment">-- this would be trivial in agda due to definitional η for records</a>
<a id="7023" class="Comment">-- so Capriotti defined a product type without η:</a>
<a id="7073" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="×-Def₂"></a><a id="7080" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7080" class="Module">×-Def₂</a> <a id="7087" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="7096" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="×-Def₂._×_"></a><a id="7101" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7101" class="Datatype Operator">_×_</a> <a id="7105" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7106" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7106" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="7108" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7108" class="Bound">j</a><a id="7109" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="7111" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7111" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="7113" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7115" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="7119" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7106" class="Bound">i</a><a id="7120" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="7122" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7122" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="7124" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7126" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="7130" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7108" class="Bound">j</a><a id="7131" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7133" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7135" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="7139" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7140" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7106" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="7142" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="7144" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7108" class="Bound">j</a><a id="7145" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7147" class="Keyword">where</a>
    <a id="×-Def₂._×_._,_"></a><a id="7157" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7157" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a> <a id="7161" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7163" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7111" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="7165" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7167" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7122" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="7169" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7171" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7111" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="7173" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7101" class="Datatype Operator">×</a> <a id="7175" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7122" class="Bound">B</a>

        <a id="7919" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7921" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7892" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7923" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#731" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="7925" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7894" class="Bound">w</a> <a id="7927" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7929" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7902" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="7931" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#731" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="7933" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7904" class="Bound">z</a> <a id="7935" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7937" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7938" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7892" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7940" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7157" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="7942" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7902" class="Bound">y</a><a id="7943" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7945" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#731" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="7947" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7948" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7894" class="Bound">w</a> <a id="7950" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7157" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="7952" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7904" class="Bound">z</a><a id="7953" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="7957" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7869" class="Function">pair=</a> <a id="7963" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#779" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="7968" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#779" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="7973" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7975" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#779" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The induction principle for the product type:

<p class="equation">
$$\mathsf{ind}_{A\times B} : \prod\limits_{C : A \times B \to \mathcal{U}}
  \left( \prod\limits_{x:A}\ \prod\limits_{y:B}\ \,C( (x,y) ) \right)
  \to \prod\limits_{x:A \times B}\ \,C(x)
$$
</p>

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="8269" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="×-Ind₂"></a><a id="8276" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#8276" class="Module">×-Ind₂</a> <a id="8283" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8284" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#8284" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="8286" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#8286" class="Bound">j</a><a id="8287" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="8289" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#8289" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="8291" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8293" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="8297" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#8284" class="Bound">i</a><a id="8298" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="8300" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#8300" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="8302" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8304" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="8308" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#8286" class="Bound">j</a><a id="8309" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8311" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="8690" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#8546" class="Function">ind-β</a> <a id="8696" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#8696" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="8698" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#8698" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="8700" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#8700" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="8702" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#8702" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="8704" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8706" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#779" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

<p class="exercise">
Generalize $$\mathsf{uniq}_{A\times B}$$ to Σ-types, and do the same for
$$\Sigma$$-types, i.e. show induction and verify the definitional equality
is valid.
</p>

Σ-type definition using `data`:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="8954" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Σ-Def₂"></a><a id="8961" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#8961" class="Module">Σ-Def₂</a> <a id="8968" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="9649" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9546" class="Function">ind</a> <a id="9653" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9653" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="9655" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9655" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="9657" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9658" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9658" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="9660" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9040" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="9662" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9662" class="Bound">b</a><a id="9663" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9665" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9667" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9655" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="9669" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9658" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="9671" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9662" class="Bound">b</a>

          <a id="9720" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9722" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9723" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9723" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="9725" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9727" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9728" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9728" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9730" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9732" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9469" class="Bound">A</a><a id="9733" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="9735" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9735" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="9737" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9739" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9480" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="9741" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9728" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9742" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9744" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9746" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9685" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="9748" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9749" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9728" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9751" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9040" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="9753" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9735" class="Bound">y</a><a id="9754" class="Symbol">))</a>

          <a id="9797" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9799" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9800" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9546" class="Function">ind</a> <a id="9804" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9685" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="9806" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9723" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="9808" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9809" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9770" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9811" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9040" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="9813" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9778" class="Bound">y</a><a id="9814" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="9817" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#731" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="9819" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9723" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="9821" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9770" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9823" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9778" class="Bound">y</a>
  <a id="9827" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9676" class="Function">ind-β</a> <a id="9833" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9833" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="9835" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9835" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="9837" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9837" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9839" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9839" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="9841" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9843" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#779" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

### Exercise 1.4

<div class="exercise">
Assuming as given only the <em>iterator</em> for natural numbers
<p class="equation">
$$\mathsf{ite} : \prod\limits_{C:\mathcal{U}} C \to (C \to C) \to \mathbb{N} \to C $$
</p>
with the defining equations
<p class="equation">
$$
\begin{align*}
\mathsf{ite}(C,c_0,c_s,0)               &\equiv c_0, \\
\mathsf{ite}(C,c_0,c_s,\mathsf{suc}(n)) &\equiv c_s(\mathsf{ite}(C,c_0,c_s,n)),
\end{align*}
$$
</p>
derive a function having the type of the recursor $$\mathsf{rec}$$.
Show that the defining equations of the recursor hold propositionally for this
function, using the induction principle for $$\mathbb{N}$$.
</div>

To solve this problem, let us define the recursor and also the induction principle
for natural numbers. (See more details about these functions in
[Induction on Natural Numbers]({% post_url 2018-02-12-induction-on-natural-numbers %})).

       <a id="11110" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11112" class="Symbol">(∀</a> <a id="11115" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11116" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11116" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="11118" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11120" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10794" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="11121" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11123" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11125" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11033" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="11127" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11116" class="Bound">n</a><a id="11128" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="11159" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11024" class="Function">ind</a> <a id="11163" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11163" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="11165" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11165" class="Bound">c₀</a> <a id="11168" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11168" class="Bound">cₛ</a> <a id="11171" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11172" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10825" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a> <a id="11176" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11176" class="Bound">n</a><a id="11177" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11179" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11181" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11168" class="Bound">cₛ</a> <a id="11184" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11176" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="11186" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11187" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11024" class="Function">ind</a> <a id="11191" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11163" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="11193" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11165" class="Bound">c₀</a> <a id="11196" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11168" class="Bound">cₛ</a> <a id="11199" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11176" class="Bound">n</a><a id="11200" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Now, we define the iterator following the equations above:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="11287" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="ℕ-Fun"></a><a id="11294" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11294" class="Module">ℕ-Fun</a> <a id="11300" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="11308" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="11313" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10774" class="Module">ℕ-Def</a> <a id="11319" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="11325" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11326" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10794" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="11327" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="11329" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10812" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a><a id="11333" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="11335" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10825" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a><a id="11338" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="11342" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="11347" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10846" class="Module">ℕ-Rec</a> <a id="11353" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="11359" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11360" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10873" class="Function">rec</a><a id="11363" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="ℕ-Fun.ite"></a><a id="11368" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11368" class="Function">ite</a> <a id="11372" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11374" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="11376" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11377" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11377" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="11379" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11381" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="11384" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11386" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11388" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11377" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="11390" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11392" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11393" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11377" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="11395" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11397" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11377" class="Bound">C</a><a id="11398" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11400" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11402" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10794" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="11404" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11406" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11377" class="Bound">C</a>
  <a id="11410" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11368" class="Function">ite</a> <a id="11414" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11414" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="11416" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11416" class="Bound">c₀</a> <a id="11419" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11419" class="Bound">cₛ</a> <a id="11422" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10812" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a>    <a id="11430" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11432" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11416" class="Bound">c₀</a>
  <a id="11437" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11368" class="Function">ite</a> <a id="11441" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11441" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="11443" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11443" class="Bound">c₀</a> <a id="11446" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11446" class="Bound">cₛ</a> <a id="11449" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11450" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10825" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a> <a id="11454" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11454" class="Bound">n</a><a id="11455" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11457" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11459" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11446" class="Bound">cₛ</a> <a id="11462" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11463" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11368" class="Function">ite</a> <a id="11467" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11441" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="11469" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11443" class="Bound">c₀</a> <a id="11472" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11446" class="Bound">cₛ</a> <a id="11475" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11454" class="Bound">n</a><a id="11476" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Then, we now can define the recursor using this `ite` by iterating over the type
`ℕ × C` (*reloading recursion*?).


<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="11620" class="Comment">-- recursor</a>
  <a id="11634" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="11639" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7080" class="Module">×-Def₂</a> <a id="11646" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="11652" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11653" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7101" class="Datatype Operator">_×_</a><a id="11656" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="11658" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7180" class="Function">proj₁</a><a id="11663" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="11665" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7261" class="Function">proj₂</a><a id="11670" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="11672" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7157" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a><a id="11675" class="Symbol">)</a>

      <a id="11756" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11757" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11368" class="Function">ite</a> <a id="11761" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11762" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10794" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="11764" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7101" class="Datatype Operator">×</a> <a id="11766" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11738" class="Bound">C</a><a id="11767" class="Symbol">)</a>

           <a id="11803" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="11806" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11807" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11807" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="11809" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11811" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10794" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="11813" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7101" class="Datatype Operator">×</a> <a id="11815" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11738" class="Bound">C</a><a id="11816" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11818" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11820" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11821" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10825" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a> <a id="11825" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11826" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7180" class="Function">proj₁</a> <a id="11832" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11807" class="Bound">p</a><a id="11833" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11835" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7157" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="11837" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11743" class="Bound">cₛ</a> <a id="11840" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11841" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7180" class="Function">proj₁</a> <a id="11847" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11807" class="Bound">p</a><a id="11848" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11850" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11851" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7261" class="Function">proj₂</a> <a id="11857" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11807" class="Bound">p</a><a id="11858" class="Symbol">)))</a>
           <a id="11873" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11746" class="Bound">n</a><a id="11874" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Now, we need to establish the propositional equality between these two
definitions of recursor, i.e, between `rec` and `rec₂`. Let's use
induction to prove that.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="12064" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="ex1-4"></a><a id="12071" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12071" class="Module">ex1-4</a> <a id="12077" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="12120" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="12125" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10846" class="Module">ℕ-Rec</a> <a id="12131" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="12137" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12138" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10873" class="Function">rec</a><a id="12141" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="12202" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="12207" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7080" class="Module">×-Def₂</a> <a id="12214" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="12220" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12221" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7101" class="Datatype Operator">_×_</a><a id="12224" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="12226" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7180" class="Function">proj₁</a><a id="12231" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="12233" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7261" class="Function">proj₂</a><a id="12238" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="12240" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7157" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a><a id="12243" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="12247" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="12252" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7419" class="Module">×-Fun₂</a>

  <a id="ex1-4.proof"></a><a id="12262" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12262" class="Function">proof</a> <a id="12268" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12270" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12271" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12271" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="12273" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12275" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="12278" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="12280" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12280" class="Bound">c₀</a> <a id="12283" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12285" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12271" class="Bound">C</a><a id="12286" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="12288" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12288" class="Bound">cₛ</a> <a id="12291" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12293" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10794" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="12295" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12297" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12271" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="12299" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12301" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12271" class="Bound">C</a><a id="12302" class="Symbol">)</a>
        <a id="12312" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12314" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="12316" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12317" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw ### Exercise 1.5

<div class="exercise">

Show that if we define

  $$A+B :\equiv \sum\limits_{(x : \mathbbbold{2})} \mathsf{rec}_{\mathbbbold{2}} (\mathcal{U}, A , B, x),$$

then we can give a definition of $$\ind\limits_{A + B}$$ for which the
definitional equalities holds.

</div>

To solve this problem, let us introduce the $$\mathcal{2}$$ type, that is, the
type with two constructors also called **Bool**. The constructors are also called
false and true respectively.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="13314" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="𝟚-Def₁"></a><a id="13321" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13321" class="Module">𝟚-Def₁</a> <a id="13328" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="13337" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="𝟚-Def₁.𝟚"></a><a id="13342" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13342" class="Datatype">𝟚</a> <a id="13344" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13346" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="13350" class="Keyword">where</a>
    <a id="𝟚-Def₁.𝟚.𝟘"></a><a id="13360" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13360" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟘</a> <a id="13362" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13364" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13342" class="Datatype">𝟚</a>
    <a id="𝟚-Def₁.𝟚.𝟙"></a><a id="13370" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13370" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟙</a> <a id="13372" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13374" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13342" class="Datatype">𝟚</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


With the recursor:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="13422" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="𝟚-Rec₁"></a><a id="13429" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13429" class="Module">𝟚-Rec₁</a> <a id="13436" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="13445" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="13450" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13321" class="Module">𝟚-Def₁</a>  <a id="13458" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="13464" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13465" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13360" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟘</a><a id="13466" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="13467" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13370" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟙</a><a id="13468" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="13469" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13342" class="Datatype">𝟚</a><a id="13470" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="𝟚-Rec₁.rec"></a><a id="13475" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13475" class="Function">rec</a> <a id="13479" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13481" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="13483" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13484" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13484" class="Bound">i</a><a id="13485" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="13487" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13488" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13488" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="13490" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13492" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="13496" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13484" class="Bound">i</a><a id="13497" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="13499" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13500" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13500" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="13502" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13504" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13488" class="Bound">C</a><a id="13505" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13507" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13508" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13508" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="13510" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13512" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13488" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="13514" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13516" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13518" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13342" class="Datatype">𝟚</a> <a id="13520" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13522" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13488" class="Bound">C</a>
  <a id="13526" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13475" class="Function">rec</a> <a id="13530" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13530" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="13532" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13532" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="13534" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13360" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟘</a> <a id="13536" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13538" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13530" class="Bound">a</a>
  <a id="13542" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13475" class="Function">rec</a> <a id="13546" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13546" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="13548" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13548" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="13550" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13370" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟙</a> <a id="13552" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13554" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13548" class="Bound">b</a>
  <a id="13558" class="Comment">-- rec is the same if_then_else</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

and its induction principle:

Now, let's try to define the recursor for this coproduct, and later,
we'll try the dependent version of it to complete the exercise.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="14404" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="+-Rec₁"></a><a id="14411" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14411" class="Module">+-Rec₁</a> <a id="14418" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="14427" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="14432" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13876" class="Module">+-Def₁</a> <a id="14439" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="14445" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14446" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13996" class="Function Operator">_+_</a><a id="14449" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="14451" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14131" class="Function">inl</a><a id="14454" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="14455" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14189" class="Function">inr</a><a id="14458" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="14459" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#5013" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a><a id="14462" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="14466" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="14471" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13321" class="Module">𝟚-Def₁</a> <a id="14478" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="14484" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14485" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13360" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟘</a><a id="14486" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="14487" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13370" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟙</a><a id="14488" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="14489" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13342" class="Datatype">𝟚</a><a id="14490" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="+-Rec₁.rec"></a><a id="14495" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14495" class="Function">rec</a> <a id="14499" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14501" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="14503" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14504" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14504" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="14506" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14506" class="Bound">j</a><a id="14507" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14509" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14510" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14510" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14512" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14512" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="14514" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14516" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="14520" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14504" class="Bound">i</a><a id="14521" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14523" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14524" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14524" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="14526" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14528" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="14532" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14506" class="Bound">j</a><a id="14533" class="Symbol">}</a>
      <a id="14541" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14543" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14544" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14510" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14546" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14548" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14524" class="Bound">C</a><a id="14549" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="14557" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14559" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14560" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14512" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="14562" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14564" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14524" class="Bound">C</a><a id="14565" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="14573" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14575" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14510" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14577" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13996" class="Function Operator">+</a> <a id="14579" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14512" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="14581" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14583" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14524" class="Bound">C</a>
  <a id="14587" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14495" class="Function">rec</a> <a id="14591" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14591" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14593" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14593" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14595" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14596" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13360" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟘</a> <a id="14598" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#5013" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="14600" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14600" class="Bound">a</a><a id="14601" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14603" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14605" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14591" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14607" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14600" class="Bound">a</a>
  <a id="14611" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14495" class="Function">rec</a> <a id="14615" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14615" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14617" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14617" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14619" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14620" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13370" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟙</a> <a id="14622" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#5013" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="14624" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14624" class="Bound">b</a><a id="14625" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14627" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14629" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14617" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14631" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14624" class="Bound">b</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Notice how the recursor of the coproduct matches with the elimination
rule of the disjunction conective also called *case analysis*. That's follows from the
[**propositions-as-types**](https://ncatlab.org/nlab/show/propositions+as+types).

![path](/assets/latexit-images/disj-elimination.png)

Finally, the induction principle for the coproduct:

### Exercise 1.6

<div class="exercise" id="ex-1.6">
Show that if we define $$A \times B :≡ \prod_{x:\mathbf{2}}\mathsf{rec}_{\mathbf{2}}\ (\mathcal{U}\, A\, B\, x)$$,
then we can give a definition of $$\mathsf{ind}_{A\times B}$$ for which the definitional
equalities propositionally (i.e. using equality types).
</div>

### Exercise 1.8

<div class="exercise" id="exercise-1.8">

Define multiplication and exponentiation using $$\mathsf{rec}{\mathbb{N}}$$.
Verify that $$(\mathbb{N},+,0,\times,1)$$ is a semiring using only
$$\ind{\mathbb{N}}$$.

</div>


<div class="proof" markdown="1">
Solution.<br/>
Operation definitions:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="17902" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Ex1-8"></a><a id="17909" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#17909" class="Module">Ex1-8</a> <a id="17915" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="17936" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="17941" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10846" class="Module">ℕ-Rec</a>

  <a id="Ex1-8.multi"></a><a id="18015" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#18015" class="Function">multi</a> <a id="18021" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18023" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="18025" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18026" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#18026" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="18028" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#18028" class="Bound">m</a> <a id="18030" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18032" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10794" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="18033" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18035" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18037" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10794" class="Datatype">ℕ</a>
  <a id="18041" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#18015" class="Function">multi</a> <a id="18047" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18049" href="{% endraw %}{% link   <a id="18128" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#18104" class="Function">exp</a> <a id="18132" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18134" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10873" class="Function">rec</a> <a id="18138" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="18140" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18147" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18149" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10794" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="18150" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18152" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="18155" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#18155" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="18157" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18159" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10825" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a> <a id="18163" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10812" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a><a id="18167" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18169" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="18172" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#18172" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="18174" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#18174" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="18176" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#18176" class="Bound">m</a> <a id="18178" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18180" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#18015" class="Function">multi</a> <a id="18186" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#18176" class="Bound">m</a> <a id="18188" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18189" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#18174" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="18191" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#18176" class="Bound">m</a><a id="18192" class="Symbol">))</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

On the other hand, a **semiring** is a type? together with two binary operators S(+,*) satisfying the following conditions:

1. Additive associativity: $$\prod_{a,b,c : S} (a+b)+c=a+(b+c)$$.

2. Additive commutativity: $$\prod_{a,b : S}  a+b=b+a$$.

3. Multiplicative associativity: $$\prod_{a,b,c : S} (a*b)*c=a*(b*c)$$.

4. Left and right distributivity:

$$\prod_{a,b,c : S} a*(b+c)=(a*b)+(a*c)\text{  and  } \prod_{a,b,c : S} (b+c)*a=(b*a)+(c*a).$$

</div>

### Exercise 1.9

<div class="exercise" id="exercise-1.9">

Define the type family $$\mathsf{Fin} : \mathbb{N} \to \mathcal{U}$$ mentioned
at the end of Section 1.3, and the dependent function $$\mathsf{fmax} :
\prod_{n:\mathbb{N}} \mathsf{Fin}(n+1)$$ mentioned in Section 1.4.
</div>

### Exercise 1.11

<div class="exercise" id="exercise-1.11">
Show that for any type $$A$$, we have $$\neg\neg\neg A \to \neg A$$.
</div>

A propositional logic proof using [Agda-Prop](http://github.com/jonaprieto/agda-prop)
library:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="20121" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Ex1-11"></a><a id="20128" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20128" class="Module">Ex1-11</a> <a id="20135" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="20143" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="20148" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="20155" href="Data.PropFormula.html" class="Module">Data.PropFormula</a> <a id="20172" class="Number">1</a>

  <a id="Ex1-11.proof"></a><a id="20177" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20177" class="Function">proof</a> <a id="20183" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20185" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="20187" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20188" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20188" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="20189" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20191" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20192" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20192" class="Bound">A</a><a id="20193" class="Symbol">}</a>
        <a id="20203" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20205" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20188" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="20207" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1657" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="20209" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="20211" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="20213" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="20215" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20192" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="20217" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#919" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⊃</a> <a id="20219" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="20221" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20192" class="Bound">A</a>
  <a id="20225" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20177" class="Function">proof</a> <a id="20231" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20232" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20232" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="20233" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="20235" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20235" class="Bound">A</a><a id="20236" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20238" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="20244" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#3276" class="InductiveConstructor">⊃-intro</a>
      <a id="20258" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20259" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#2276" class="InductiveConstructor">¬-intro</a>
          <a id="20277" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20278" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#2387" class="InductiveConstructor">¬-elim</a>
              <a id="20299" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20300" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1868" class="InductiveConstructor">weaken</a> <a id="20307" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20235" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="20309" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20310" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1706" class="InductiveConstructor">assume</a> <a id="20317" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20318" class="Argument">Γ</a> <a id="20320" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="20322" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20232" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="20323" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20325" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20326" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="20328" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20329" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="20331" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20332" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="20334" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20235" class="Bound">A</a><a id="20335" class="Symbol">)))))</a>
              <a id="20355" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20356" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#2276" class="InductiveConstructor">¬-intro</a>
                <a id="20380" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20381" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#2387" class="InductiveConstructor">¬-elim</a>
                  <a id="20406" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20407" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1706" class="InductiveConstructor">assume</a> <a id="20414" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20415" class="Argument">Γ</a> <a id="20417" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="20419" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20232" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="20421" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1170" class="Function Operator">,</a> <a id="20423" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="20425" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="20427" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="20429" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20235" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="20431" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1170" class="Function Operator">,</a> <a id="20433" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20235" class="Bound">A</a><a id="20434" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20436" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20437" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="20439" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20235" class="Bound">A</a><a id="20440" class="Symbol">))</a>
                  <a id="20461" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20462" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1868" class="InductiveConstructor">weaken</a> <a id="20469" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20470" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="20472" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20235" class="Bound">A</a><a id="20473" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20475" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20476" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1706" class="InductiveConstructor">assume</a> <a id="20483" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20484" class="Argument">Γ</a> <a id="20486" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="20488" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20232" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="20490" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1170" class="Function Operator">,</a> <a id="20492" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="20494" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="20496" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="20498" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20235" class="Bound">A</a><a id="20499" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20501" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20235" class="Bound">A</a><a id="20502" class="Symbol">))))))</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

In type theory, the term is:

$$
λ (x : ((A → ⊥) → ⊥) → ⊥) (a : A) . x ((λ h : A → ⊥) . ha) :
((A → ⊥) → ⊥) → ⊥) → (A → ⊥)
$$

### Exercise 1.16

<div class="exercise" id="exercise-1.16">
Show that addition of natural numbers is commutative:
<p class="equation">
$$
\prod\limits_{i,j : \mathbb{N}}\ (i + j = j + i).
$$
</p>
</div>

Hint: by induction twice.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="20893" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Ex1-16"></a><a id="20900" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20900" class="Module">Ex1-16</a> <a id="20907" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="20915" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="20920" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10774" class="Module">ℕ-Def</a>
  <a id="20928" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="20933" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10997" class="Module">ℕ-Ind</a>
  <a id="20941" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="20946" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#17909" class="Module">Ex1-8</a> <a id="20952" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="20958" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20959" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#17950" class="Function Operator">_+_</a><a id="20962" class="Symbol">)</a>

## Chapter 2

### Exercise 2.6

<div class="exercise" id="exercise-2.6">
Prove that if $$p : x \equiv y$$, then the function
$$(p \cdot -) : (y \equiv z) \to (x \equiv z)$$ is an equivalence.
</div>

![path-triangle](/assets/ipe-images/path-triangle.png)

<div class="proof">
Solution. <br/>

To show the equivalence, it sufficies to show a function
$$g : x \equiv z \to y \equiv z$$ such that we can prove
$$ (p \cdot -) \circ g \sim \mathsf{id}_{x \equiv z}$$ and
$$ g \circ (p \cdot -) \sim \mathsf{id}_{y \equiv z}$$.

Let's define the function $$g$$.
<p class="equation">
$$
\begin{align*}
&g : x ≡ z → y ≡ z\\
&g~m~=~\mathsf{trans}~(\mathsf{sym}~p)~m
\end{align*}
$$
</p>
<br/>

($$(p \cdot -) \circ g \sim \mathsf{id}_{x \equiv z}$$):
Let be $$m : x ≡ z$$, we have,

<p class="equation">
$$
\begin{align*}
(p \cdot -) \circ g (m) &= (p \cdot -)~(g~m)\\
                        &= (p \cdot -)~(\mathsf{trans}~(\mathsf{sym}~p)~m)\\
                        &= \mathsf{trans}~p~(\mathsf{trans}~(\mathsf{sym}~p)~m)\\
                        &= \mathsf{trans}~(\mathsf{trans}~p~(\mathsf{sym}~p))~m\\
                        &= \mathsf{trans}~\mathsf{refl}_{x≡z}~m\\
                        &= m
\end{align*}
$$
</p>
<br/>
($$ g \circ (p \cdot -) \sim \mathsf{id}_{y \equiv z}$$):
Let be $$n : y ≡ z$$, we have,

<p class="equation">
$$
\begin{align*}
g \circ (p \cdot -) n &= g (\mathsf{trans}~p~n)\\
                      &= (\mathsf{trans}~(\mathsf{sym}~p)~(\mathsf{trans}~p~n)\\
                      &= \mathsf{trans}~(\mathsf{trans}~(\mathsf{sym}~p)~p)~n\\
                      &= \mathsf{trans}~\mathsf{refl}_{y ≡ z}~n\\
                      &= n.
\end{align*}
$$
</p>

</div>


### Exercise 2.10

<div class="exercise" id="exercise-2.10">
Prove that ∑-types are associative, in that for any $$A : \mathcal{U}$$
and families $$B : A  \to U$$ and $$C : \sum_{(x : A)} B(x) \to \mathcal{U}$$,
we have
<p class="equation">
$$\sum\limits_{(x : A)} \sum\limits_{(y : B(x))} C((x,y)) \simeq \sum\limits_{p : \sum_{x:A} B(x)} C(p)$$.
</p>
</div>

<div class="proof" id="proof-2.10">
Solution.<br/>
We can prove that the following functions $$f$$ and $$g$$ are inverses.

<p class="equation">
$$\sum\limits_{(x : A)} \sum\limits_{(y : B(x))} C((x,y)) \overset{f}{\underset{g}{\rightleftarrows}} \sum\limits_{p : \sum_{x:A} B(x)} C(p)$$.
</p>
defined by $$f(a,b,c) :\equiv ((a,b),c)$$ and $$g(z,c) :\equiv (\mathsf{proj}_1 z,\mathsf{proj}_{2} z, c)$$.<br/>
Indeed,
<p class="equation">
$$
\begin{align*}
(f \circ g) (z, c) &:\equiv f (g (z,c))\\
&:\equiv f\,(\mathsf{proj}_1 z,\mathsf{proj}_{2} z, c)\\
&:\equiv ((\mathsf{proj}_1 z,\mathsf{proj}_{2} z), c)
\end{align*}
$$
</p>
</div>

  <a id="24451" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="24456" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4918" class="Module">Σ-Def₁</a> <a id="24463" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="24469" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24470" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#5033" class="Field">proj₁</a><a id="24475" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="24477" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#5049" class="Field">proj₂</a><a id="24482" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="24484" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#5013" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a><a id="24487" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="24488" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4941" class="Record">Σ</a><a id="24489" class="Symbol">)</a>
